  <div class="step">

    <header class="step__header" data-attribute="title"><h5>Philanthropy Step 1 of 2:</h5>
</header> <!-- .form step header -->

    <div class="step__description" data-attribute="description">
<p>Chipotle supports organizations in a variety of ways, including in-restaurant <a href="http://www.chipotle.com/fundraisers"><span style="color:#c08c19">fundraisers</span></a> for schools, <a href="https://www.chipotle.com/reading"><span style="color:#c08c19">reading rewards</span></a> for libraries and schools, in-kind donations, and our <a href="http://www.shopwithscrip.com/Learn?banneroverride=chpo&amp;refID=chpo" target="_blank"><span style="color:#c08c19">Scrip</span></a> program. We are exclusively focused on assisting:</p>

<ul>
	<li>K-12 Schools </li>
	<li>Libraries</li>
	<li>Youth Community Groups</li>
	<li>Community Gardens</li>
	<li>Food and Sustainable Agriculture Groups</li>
	<li>University Groups</li>
</ul>

<p>If your request falls into one of these categories and meets the following guidelines, please submit an application on the next page. Due to the large number of requests we receive, we cannot honor all of them. If your request is approved, we will contact you soon.</p>

<h5>Application</h5>

<p>Please complete the online application form at the link below. We will not review applications submitted via email or hard copy.</p>

<h5>Minimum Lead Time</h5>

<p>Requests must be received at least 6 weeks prior to the event/donation date in order to be considered.</p>

<h5>Eligibility</h5>

<p>Because of our strategy of proactive, long term engagement, we are no longer accepting un-solicited requests for sponsorship. We will also not provide charitable support for organizations in the following categories:</p>

<ul>
	<li>Individuals (scholarships, stipends, fellowships, personal assistance); </li>
	<li>For-profit ventures;</li>
	<li>Religious groups for religious purposes;</li>
	<li>Capital campaigns, endowment funds or memorials;</li>
	<li>Lobbying, political or fraternal activities; </li>
	<li>Individual study, research or travel grants</li>
</ul>

<h5>Discrimination</h5>

<p>Chipotle will not support organizations that discriminate against a person or a group on the basis of age, political affiliation, race, national origin, ethnicity, gender, disability, sexual orientation or religious belief.</p>

    <div class="section__description" data-attribute="description">
<h5>Reading Rewards Requests</h5>

<p>We’re passionate about more than perfectly rolled burritos. At Chipotle, we’re also committed to helping young minds grow. To help motivate young readers, we provide Chipotle Reading Rewards, so you can reward book smarts with delicious food crafted from real, whole ingredients. </p>

<h5>WHAT ARE CHIPOTLE READING REWARDS?</h5>

<p>Chipotle Reading Rewards are FREE kid's meal cards that can be used as incentives for your school or library’s reading program - here’s how it works.</p>

<ul>
	<li>Apply for Chipotle Reading Rewards</li>
	<li>Kick off your reading program</li>
	<li>Reward your readers with free Chipotle</li>
</ul>

<h5>DON'T HAVE A READING REWARDS PROGRAM IN PLACE?</h5>

<p>Your school or library can still participate in Chipotle Reading Rewards. You can either create a challenge with your fellow teachers, librarians, and educational staff or you can try ours.</p>

<ul>
	<li>Approved applicants will be emailed a custom <a href="https://chipotle.com/readinglog2017" target="_blank"><span style="color: rgb(192, 140, 25);">Reading Log</span></a>
</li>
	<li>Ask your readers to color in each day they have read 10-20 minutes</li>
	<li>Reward your readers with free Chipotle</li>
</ul>
</div> <!-- .form section description -->

    <div class="section__body" data-attribute="content"></div> <!-- .section body -->

  </div> <!-- .section -->

<h5>School Applicants</h5>

	<li>Decide when your school’s reading challenge will conclude so that we send you the appropriate expiration date on the reading rewards. Note that quantities are limited while supplies last.</li>
	<li>Be prepared to use a valid school email address and request the cards to ship directly to the school or district.</li>
	<li>Submit the application.</li>
</ul>

Offer good at participating Chipotle locations only. Additional restrictions may apply.</p>

	<li>Submit the application.</li>
</ul>

    <header class="step__header" data-attribute="title"></header> <!-- .form step header -->

    <div class="step__description" data-attribute="description">
<h5>Becoming a Supplier Step 1 of 2:</h5>

<p>If you have meat, vegetables or other ingredients and products that you would like to supply Chipotle, please review the criteria on this page and provide your information through the link below.</p>

<p>We will answer you with many thanks and send along your information to our purchasing team. Keep in mind that we have a certain set of ingredients on our menus and we may not be looking for additional suppliers at this point in time. We will however keep all of your information on hand as our needs grow in the future.</p>

<h5>General Needs</h5>

<ul>
	<li>
<strong>Meat </strong>Naturally Raised Beef, Chicken and Pork (certain cuts)</li>
	<li>
<strong>Dairy </strong>Cheese and Sour Cream</li>
	<li>
<strong>Produce, Beans &amp; Rice </strong>Avocados, Beans (Black &amp; Pinto), Bell Peppers, Cilantro, Jalapenos, Limes, Lemons, Red Onions, Rice (White &amp; Brown), Romaine Lettuce, Tomatoes</li>
	<li><strong>Beverages</strong></li>
	<li><strong>Paper &amp; Packaging</strong></li>
	<li><strong>Other Food Ingredients </strong></li>
</ul>

<h5>Requirements</h5>

<ul>
	<li>Ability to follow the guidelines of our <a href="http://chipotle.com/food-with-integrity">Food With Integrity</a> program, which includes our requirements and goals for food safety, animal welfare, sustainability and social accountability</li>
	<li>Willingness to provide detailed information about the practices on your farm or ranch, and the practices in your production facilities</li>
	<li>Currently using processing facilities that have been registered and inspected by the USDA or FDA, and that have been inspected or certified for food safety by an accredited 3rd party (or the willingness and ability to switch to such a facility)</li>
	<li>Produce growers should also maintain a written food safety program that includes Good Management Practices (GMPs) or Good Agricultural Practices (GAPs), as well as a current GMP or GAP audit with a passing score</li>
	<li>Willingness to host periodic visits by our team to see your practices and facilities first hand</li>
	<li>Eagerness to improve your practices year over year</li>
</ul>
</div> <!-- .form step description -->
